the provided manifests and returns a slice of file instances with appropriate\n// content type extensions.\nfunc (s *Store) fetchFiles(ctx context.Context, store oras.ReadOnlyTarget, manifest v1.Manifest) ([]fs.File, error) {\n\tvar files []fs.File\n\n\tcreated, err := time.Parse(time.RFC3339, manifest.Annotations[v1.AnnotationCreated])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor layer,\n\t\t\t\tencoding: encoding,\n\t\t\t\tmod:      created,\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn files, nil\n}\n\n// Bundle is a record of an existing Flipt feature bundle\ntype Bundle struct context.Context) (bundles []Bundle, _ error) {\n\tfi, err := os.Open(s.opts.bundleDir)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\tdefer fi.Close()\n\n\tentries, err := fi.ReadDir(-1)\n\tif err manifest.Annotations[v1.AnnotationRefName],\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tbundle.CreatedAt, err = parseCreated(man.Annotations)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tbundles = directory, instead use one of the function options\n// e.g. WithBundleDir or WithCredentials\ntype StoreOptions struct {\n\tbundleDir       string\n\tmanifestVersion oras.PackManifestVersion\n\tauth            *struct {\n\t\tusername string\n\t\tpassword string\n\t}\n\tawsProvider *struct {\n\t\tenabled  bool\n\t\tfallback *struct {\n\t\t\tusername string\n\t\t\tpassword string\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// {\n\tregistry.Reference\n\tScheme string\n}\n\nfunc ParseReference(repository string) (Reference, error) {\n\tscheme, repository, match := strings.Cut(repository, \"://\")\n\t// support empty scheme {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01AUfjZGreH3s1MH5cttgWsP","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01HBxwCodV2pSqixFdrmxhTX","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/flipt/internal/config/testdata/storage/oci_aws_example.md","content":"# OCI Storage with AWS ECR Authentication\n\nThis example demonstrates how to configure Flipt to use AWS ECR (Elastic Container Registry) for storing OCI bundles with automatic credential refreshing via the AWS credentials chain.\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Using AWS Credentials Chain Only\n\nWhen AWS credentials are available through environment variables, IAM roles, or other methods supported by the AWS SDK v2, you can enable the AWS provider:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: 123456789.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/flipt-bundles:latest\n    bundles_directory: /path/to/bundles\n    authentication:\n      aws_provider:\n        enabled: true\n    poll_interval: 30s\n```\n\n### With Fallback Credentials\n\nFor cases where AWS credentials might not be available in some environments, you can provide fallback static credentials:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: 123456789.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/flipt-bundles:latest\n    bundles_directory: /path/to/bundles\n    authentication:\n      username: fallback_user\n      password: fallback_password\n      aws_provider:\n        enabled: true\n    poll_interval: 30s\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. **AWS Credentials Chain**: When `aws_provider.enabled` is set to `true`, Flipt will attempt to load AWS credentials from the AWS credentials chain.\n2. **Fallback**: If AWS credentials are not available, the static username/password credentials (if provided) will be used as a fallback.\n3. **Auto-Refresh**: The AWS credentials chain automatically handles token refresh, so Flipt can continuously pull bundles without manual intervention even after token expiry.\n\n## AWS Credentials Sources\n\nThe AWS SDK v2 supports credentials from multiple sources (in order of precedence):\n1. Environment variables (`AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `AWS_SESSION_TOKEN`)\n2. Shared credentials file (`~/.aws/credentials`)\n3. Shared config file (`~/.aws/config`)\n4. IAM role (when running on EC2, ECS, Lambda, etc.)\n5. Container credentials (ECS task credentials)\n\n## Benefits\n\n- **No Manual Intervention**: Credentials are automatically refreshed as needed\n- **Flexible**: Works with different AWS credential sources\n- **Backward Compatible**: Falls back to static credentials if AWS credentials are not available\n- **Secure**: IAM roles are supported, reducing the need to manage static credentials\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":457,"cache_read_input_tokens":83654,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":457},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"35eafb3c-0d40-431e-96fe-92ff85c8c4c5","uuid":"b977965f-9e3d-4b55-869c-f9644cb402ce"}

OCI Storage with AWS ECR Authentication\n\nThis example demonstrates how to configure Flipt to use AWS ECR (Elastic Container Registry) for storing OCI bundles with automatic credential refreshing via the AWS credentials chain.\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Using AWS Credentials Chain Only\n\nWhen AWS credentials are available through environment variables, IAM roles, or other methods supported by the AWS SDK v2, you can enable the AWS provider:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: 123456789.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/flipt-bundles:latest\n    bundles_directory: /path/to/bundles\n    authentication:\n      aws_provider:\n        enabled: true\n    poll_interval: 30s\n```\n\n### With Fallback Credentials\n\nFor cases where AWS credentials might not be available in some environments, you can provide fallback static credentials:\n\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  type: oci\n  oci:\n    repository: 123456789.dkr.ecr.us-east-1.amazonaws.com/flipt-bundles:latest\n    bundles_directory: /path/to/bundles\n    authentication:\n      username: fallback_user\n      password: fallback_password\n      aws_provider:\n        enabled: true\n    poll_interval: 30s\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n1. **AWS Credentials Chain**: When `aws_provider.enabled` is set to `true`, Flipt will attempt to load AWS credentials from the AWS credentials chain.\n2. **Fallback**: If AWS credentials are not available, the static username/password credentials (if provided) will be used as a fallback.\n3. **Auto-Refresh**: The AWS credentials chain automatically handles token refresh, so Flipt can continuously pull bundles without manual intervention even after token expiry.\n\n## AWS Credentials Sources\n\nThe AWS SDK v2 supports credentials from multiple sources (in order of precedence):\n1. Environment variables (`AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID`, `AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY`, `AWS_SESSION_TOKEN`)\n2. Shared credentials file (`~/.aws/credentials`)\n3. Shared config file (`~/.aws/config`)\n4. IAM role (when running on EC2, ECS, Lambda, etc.)\n5. Container credentials (ECS task credentials)\n\n## Benefits\n\n- **No Manual Intervention**: Credentials are automatically refreshed as needed\n- **Flexible**: Works with different AWS credential sources\n- **Backward Compatible**: Falls back to static credentials if AWS credentials are not available\n- **Secure**: IAM roles are supported, reducing the need to manage static credentials\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
